vicerrectoria darmasiswa scholarship program offered the indonesian government all citizen from country which indonesia diplomatic relation with study indonesian craft and other specific subject indonesian higher education institution selected various city this program organized the ministry research and technology ministry finance and the ministry foreign affair the republic the main objective the darmasiswa program increase and cultivate interest indonesian language and indonesian culture among citizen from other also designed increase mutual understanding and provide stronger cultural bond between different prospective awardees are required register and submit all document darmasiswa official website the coverage includes monthly living allowance that will received idr book allowance idr and settlement allowance idr awardees will also provided with accommodation and transportation during the orientation program their time arrival aligns with the schedule provided the awardees are advised bring extra money for their personal unforeseen expense the scholarship open foreign national who have completed secondary education it with minimum age year and maximum age limit year for this prospective awardees should able communicate english english language proficiency other certificate good health proven medical and have basic knowledge and strong interest the applied the complete information about the including the required document and application available sunday april the further information for colombian seccion sociocultura indonesia vicerrectoria vicerrectoria darmasiswa scholarship program offered the indonesian government all citizen from country which indonesia diplomatic relation with study indonesian craft and other specific subject indonesian higher education institution selected various city this program organized the ministry research and technology ministry finance and the ministry foreign affair the republic the main objective the darmasiswa program increase and cultivate interest indonesian language and indonesian culture among citizen from other also designed increase mutual understanding and provide stronger cultural bond between different prospective awardees are required register and submit all document darmasiswa official website the coverage includes monthly living allowance that will received idr book allowance idr and settlement allowance idr awardees will also provided with accommodation and transportation during the orientation program their time arrival aligns with the schedule provided the awardees are advised bring extra money for their personal unforeseen expense the scholarship open foreign national who have completed secondary education it with minimum age year and maximum age limit year for this prospective awardees should able communicate english english language proficiency other certificate good health proven medical and have basic knowledge and strong interest the applied the complete information about the including the required document and application available sunday april the further information for colombian seccion sociocultura indonesia vicerrectoria vicerrectoria darmasiswa scholarship program offered the indonesian government all citizen from country which indonesia diplomatic relation with study indonesian craft and other specific subject indonesian higher education institution selected various city this program organized the ministry research and technology ministry finance and the ministry foreign affair the republic the main objective the darmasiswa program increase and cultivate interest indonesian language and indonesian culture among citizen from other also designed increase mutual understanding and provide stronger cultural bond between different prospective awardees are required register and submit all document darmasiswa official website the coverage includes monthly living allowance that will received idr book allowance idr and settlement allowance idr awardees will also provided with accommodation and transportation during the orientation program their time arrival aligns with the schedule provided the awardees are advised bring extra money for their personal unforeseen expense the scholarship open foreign national who have completed secondary education it with minimum age year and maximum age limit year for this prospective awardees should able communicate english english language proficiency other certificate good health proven medical and have basic knowledge and strong interest the applied the complete information about the including the required document and application available sunday april the further information for colombian seccion sociocultura indonesia vicerrectoria
